'Copyright © 2014, 2016, 2018 Monotype Imaging Inc. All rights reserved'
Please verify against spec. It should follow this structure:
'Copyright (c) XXXX - XXXX /entity/. All rights reserved.'

Posterama Regular (posterama-regular.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Posterama', Everything looks good.

Pass

'space' in NID 6 cause issues in fontbook for Mac.

NID 6 is 'Posterama', Everything looks good.

Posterama Bold Italic (posterama-bolditalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Posterama-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

name

Mac NID 6

'space' in NID 6 cause issues in fontbook for Mac.

NID 6 is 'Posterama-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Pass

Posterama Regular (posterama-regular.ttf)

GPOS

kern

Simple check if kern feature in GPOS table.

The font has GPOS kerning.

Warning

Posterama Regular (posterama-regular.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in TTF font.

Font has 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.
For example: PowerPoint only supports a flat GPOS kerning or a kern table. So, if the customer requires PowerPoint support, a kern table is necessary.
